<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/mahwig3172/djy/blob/master/gb/21/9/7/n13215952.md#1" target="_blank">持续更新：亚省“中共病毒”疫情一览（七）</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/mahwig3172/djy/blob/master/gb/21/9/7/n13215952.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2021/08/id13151379-shutterstock2_1880185900-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>【更新】9月28日（周二），亚省报告了1,246例中共病毒（COVID-19）新病例。有18人死亡。死亡总人数为2,663人。
